***veulen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veulen.html>veulen</a> (20913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">volen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*folīn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fulīną</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fulô</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">foal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fohlen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veulen.html>veulen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veulens.html>veulens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veulentje.html>veulentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A foal, the young of any equine and some other quadrupeds, either colt (male) or filly (female); unless specified, usually a horse's</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A young person, especially behaving naively; fool</li></ol>

***vezel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vezel.html>vezel</a> (25528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*vesele</i> (from which <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">veselen</i>), from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vese</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-ele</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijzen.html>vees</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-el</i>.  Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fasōn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fiber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">faso</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vezel.html>vezel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vezels.html>vezels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vezeltje.html>vezeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fibre <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Commonwealth</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; fiber <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">single piece/<a href = vnd.unilang:strand.html>strand</a> of fabric or other material</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>A dietary fibre.</li></ol>

***via.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> (890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">viā</i>, the ablative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">road, way</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin, plausibly cognate with <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vehere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to conduct</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Entered Dutch in the Latin phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">per <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">by way of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, after the Portuguese <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt"><a href = vnd.unilang:por.html>por</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_3">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a></a>, through, by way of</li>
<li>by (means of); using (a medium).</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">through (by way of)</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:langs.html>langs</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">by (means of)</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">per</span></li></ul>
</body>

***viceroy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:viceroy.html>viceroy</a> (34563)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">vice-roy</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">vice-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:roy.html>roy</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">king</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:viceroy.html>viceroy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">viceroys</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who governs a country, province, or colony as the representative of a monarch.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">vicar</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">provost</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Ireland <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> governed by a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:viceroy.html>Viceroy</a></b> representing the English King/Queen when it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> part of the United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1980</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_Lean" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:David Lean">David Lean</a>, <i>A Screenplay of E.M. <a href = vnd.unilang:forster.html>Forster</a>'s A Passage to India</i>, Script City, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=EDnyAAAAMAAJamp;q=%22the+viceroy%27s+on+board%22amp;dq=%22the+viceroy%27s+on+board%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ved=0ahUKEwjg7Zuwj5HbAhXLurwKHSX8AzAQ6AEIMTAC">page 2</a>,
<dl><dd>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:viceroy.html>Viceroy</a>'</b>s on board <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> tends to liven <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> up.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A zongdu.</li>
<li>An orange and black North American butterfly (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Limenitis_archippus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Limenitis archippus"><i>Limenitis archippus</i></a></span>), so named because it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> similar to, but <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> than, the monarch butterfly.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">video</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-theek</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Videothek</i>, which could well be the origin of the Dutch term.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:videotheek.html>videotheek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:videotheek.html>videotheken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:videotheek.html>videotheekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:videotheek.html>videotheek</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> (412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">viuwar</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fedwōr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷetwṓr</i>, the neuter form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷetwóres</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vierdaagse.html>vierdaagse</a> (72021)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vierdaags.html>vierdaags</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vierdaagse.html>vierdaagse</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vierdaagse.html>vierdaagsen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vierdaagse.html>vierdaagses</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A four-day episodal race, contest or sports event.</li>

***viering.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:viering.html>viering</a> (14581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vieren.html>vieren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:viering.html>viering</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vieringen.html>vieringen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:viering.html>vierinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>celebration</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cross between the nave and transepts of a church</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:viering.html>viering</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>

***vies.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vies.html>vies</a> (2824)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijzen.html>vijs</a></i>, of uncertain origin. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">fies</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vies.html>vies</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:viezer.html>viezer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vies.html>vies</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:viest.html>viest</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dirty (not clean)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>Al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vies.html>vieze</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:potten.html>potten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pannen.html>pannen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bah.html>bah</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">All those <b>dirty</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:pots.html>pots</a> and pans here, bleh!</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smerig.html>smerig</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>bad-tasting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vies.html>vies</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerecht.html>gerecht</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This dish <b>tastes bad</b>!</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onsmakelijk.html>onsmakelijk</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>dirty, also in a sexual sense
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vies.html>vieze</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerel.html>kerel</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What a <b>dirty</b> guy!</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijfde.html>vijfde</a> (3046)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vijfte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fīfto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fimftô</i>.
</p>

</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hoofdtelwoord"><i>Hoofdtelwoord</i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijfling.html>vijfling</a> (62423)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijf.html>vijf</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">five</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ling</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijfling.html>vijfling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijfling.html>vijflingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijfling.html>vijflingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>quintuplet; one of a group of five <a href = vnd.unilang:babies.html>babies</a> born from the same mother during the same birth.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vijfling.html>vijfling</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:vijf.html>vijf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> één <a href = vnd.unilang:zwangerschap.html>zwangerschap</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:dracht.html>dracht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geboren.html>geboren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a></li></ol>

***vijftien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijftien.html>vijftien</a> (2075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijftien.html>vijftien</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*vīftēn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*vīftien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fimftehun</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">fyftjin</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">fünfzehn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fifteen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">femten</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***vijftig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijftig.html>vijftig</a> (2235)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vijftich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fīftig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fimf tigiwiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijftig.html>vijftig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>fifty</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although <a href = vnd.unilang:spelt.html>spelt</a> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">v-</i>, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traditionally pronounced with initial <span class="IPA">/f/</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> in accents that generally do not devoice <i>v-</i>. (This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeventig.html>zeventig</a></i> ["seventy"], which used to have a prefix <i>t-</i> and hence a devoiced <i>z-</i>). However, there are also many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> who pronounce <span class="IPA">/v/</span> in line with the spelling as a hypercorrection.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hoofdtelwoord"><i>Hoofdtelwoord</i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vigeboom</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fīgbōm</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijver.html>vijver</a> (8777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">viver</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">vivier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vīvārium</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> merged with or replaced <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wuwer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*wiwer</i>, an older borrowing directly from Latin; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weiher</i>.
